<span data-ttu-id="e0e91-1612">Esta clase contiene los siguientes atributos para Windows Server 2008 R2:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e0e91-1612">This class contains the following attributes for Windows Server 2008 R2:</span></span>

| <span data-ttu-id="e0e91-1954">Entrada</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e0e91-1954">Entry</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="e0e91-1955">Value</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e0e91-1955">Value</span></span> |
